<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кулинария.html>кулинари́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kulinaríja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кулинария.html>кулина́рия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kulinárija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:культивировать.html>культиви́ровать</a> (25414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kultivieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:культовый.html>ку́льтовый</a> (21580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:культ.html>культ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kulʹt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:культовый.html>ку́льтовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kúlʹtovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>religious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:культовый.html>ку́льтовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предмет.html>предме́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kúlʹtovyj</b> predmét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">object of <b>religious</b> worship</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cult
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:культовый.html>ку́льтовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фильм</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kúlʹtovyj</b> filʹm</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>cult</b> film</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:культовый.html>ку́льтовой</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó múzyka stála <b>kúlʹtovoj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his music has become something of a <b>cult</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кума.html>кума</a> (16581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кума.html>кума́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kumá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кума.html>кумы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кума.html>кумы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кума.html>кум</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кума.html>кум</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>godmother of one's child or godchild, or mother of one's godchild, gossip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> form of address to a middle-aged woman</li></ol>

***кумир.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кумир.html>куми́р</a> (8186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">кѹмиръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kumirŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whose origin is uncertain. Perhaps a Turkic<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semitic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Semitic languages">Semitic</a></span><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> borrowing: compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syriac_language" class="extiw" title="w:Syriac language">Classical Syriac</a></span> <i class="Syrc mention" lang="syc">ܟܘܡܪܐ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="syc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kūmrāʾ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">priest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence Old Armenian <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">քուրմ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kʿurm</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">priest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Has also been connected to Ossetian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="os">гуымиры</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="os-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">g°ymiry</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">giant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and Georgian <i class="Geor mention" lang="ka">გმირი</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ka-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gmiri</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hero</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and together with them derived from the name of Cimmerians.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кумир.html>куми́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kumír</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кумир.html>куми́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кумир.html>куми́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кумир.html>куми́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">paganism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> idol, graven image</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> beloved person</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идол.html>и́дол</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ídol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ку<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́р</a></b>

Зализняка).
</p>
<p><b>ку<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́р</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купать.html>купа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́льный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-álʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***купать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:купать.html>купа́ть</a> (21075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">купати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kǫpati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купать.html>купа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искупать.html>искупа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>вы́купать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bathe, to give a bath (<i>transitive only, to bathe somebody; use <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купаться.html>купа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kupátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (reflexive, intransitive) to bathe oneself</i>)</li></ol>

<p><b>ку<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>па́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:выкупать.html>выкупа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:искупать.html>искупа́ть</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:купаться.html>купа́ться</a> (4115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купать.html>купа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купаться.html>купа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kupátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выкупаться.html>вы́купаться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искупаться.html>искупа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bathe, to take a bath, to have a bath</li>
<li>to swim <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to immerse oneself, or part of the body, in water for pleasure or refreshment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:купе.html>купе</a> (5132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Liggvagnskupe.jpg/220px-Liggvagnskupe.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/c4/Liggvagnskupe.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="315" data-file-height="420" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:купе.html>купе</a></div></div></div>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">coupé</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купе.html>купе́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kupɛ́</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>compartment (chamber), couchette</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ку<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пе́ц</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 5*b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происходить.html>происхо́дит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чередование.html>чередова́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нулём</a>».

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:купечество.html>купе́чество</a> (32324)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ку<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пе́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>че<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ство</b>

***купить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a> (576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kupiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покупать.html>покупа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to buy, to purchase
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> кое-что́ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú koje-štó <b>kupítʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I want <b>to buy</b> something.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
